201→\tprivate async findLanguage(resource: vscode.Uri): Promise<LanguageProvider | undefined> {\n   202→\t\ttry {\n   203→\t\t\t// First try finding language just based on the resource.\n   204→\t\t\t// This is not strictly correct but should be in the vast majority of cases\n   205→\t\t\t// (except when someone goes and maps `.js` to `typescript` or something...)\n   206→\t\t\tfor reportUnnecessary: any; reportDeprecated: any } {\n   277→\t\tconst { start, end, text } = diagnostic;\n   278→\t\tconst range = new vscode.Range(typeConverters.Position.fromLocation(start),
